The sensor captures one frame per stage. Keep your finger flat and still.
You will be told exactly when to TOUCH and when to REMOVE.

Get ready — TOUCH finger on sensor in:

>>> TOUCH NOW <<<

This program will enroll the selected finger overwriting any print for the same finger that was enrolled previously. Fingerprint updates without erasing old data are possible on devices supporting that. Ctrl+C interrupts program execution.
Choose the finger to enroll:

  [1] left index
  [2] left middle
  [3] left ring
  [4] left little
  [5] right thumb
  [6] right index
  [7] right middle
  [8] right ring
  [9] right little
